The `Webhook` struct (line 50 in webhook.go) serves as the abstract base class for all webhook admission plugins, containing infrastructure like `ClientManager`, namespace/object matchers, and a `Dispatcher` interface. The `Dispatch` method (line 255 in webhook.go) is the core entry point that retrieves webhooks from the source and delegates to the specific dispatcher implementation. The `ShouldCallHook` method (line 158) evaluates whether a webhook should be invoked based on namespace selectors, object selectors, and match conditions.\\n\\n## Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic\\nThe mutating webhook dispatcher is implemented in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`. The key innovation is reinvocation support: the `Dispatch` method (line 105) uses a `webhookReinvokeContext` stored in the admission attributes' reinvocation context. The reinvocation logic is implemented in `mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`: when the `callAttrMutatingHook` method (line 244) modifies an object, it triggers `RequireReinvokingPreviouslyInvokedPlugins` to mark eligible webhooks (those with `IfNeededReinvocationPolicy`) for reinvocation. The reinvocation context tracks which webhooks should be reinvoked via `ShouldReinvokeWebhook` (line 35 in reinvocationcontext.go). This ensures that if earlier mutations trigger subsequent webhooks, all affected webhooks are reinvoked in a controlled manner.\\n\\n## Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch\\nThe validating webhook dispatcher is implemented in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`. The `validatingDispatcher` type (line 55) implements the `Dispatcher` interface. The key difference from mutating webhooks is parallel execution: the `Dispatch` method (line 88) uses goroutines with `sync.WaitGroup` (line 126) to spawn concurrent validation calls. It first collects all matching webhooks in a loop (lines 96-111), then launches goroutines for each webhook (lines 129-228). This allows validating webhooks to execute concurrently since they don't modify the object, improving performance.\\n\\n## WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer\\nThe `WebhookAccessor` interface (line 37 in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`) provides a unified abstraction for both mutating and validating webhooks.
